 (input bhashaa se) After the Cow Conservation Act in Gujarat, the Goseva Commission has brought tourism with cows, which aims to promote the scientificity of the cow with its religious significance, so that the cows are prevented from going to the slaughterhouse
 gujarat ke gir ke sher jahaan desh ore duniya main jane jate hai or jise dekhne ke liye salanaa lakhon paryatak gujarat aate hai, vaise hi ab gujarat main gaay ko lekar goseva ayog ne gaay tourism shuru kiya he
 Through this, people of the country and the world will get an opportunity to know and understand the Gir cow breed of Gujarat and the breed of cow cow cow
 paryatakon ko goseva ayog gir gaay kii goshaala main le jaayegaa, jahaan gir gaay kii alag-alag 18 naslon ke bare main jaankaree milegi
 The importance of not only the milk of cow's milk but also the extracts of cow urine made from it, the medicine made from cow urine and the benefits of cow's milk will be explained
 yahi nahin agar koi gaay ko apane ghar main paalna chahta he to uski bhi jaankaree yahaan muhaiyaa karwaai jaaegi
 Gopal Sutariya, the founder of Gir Ki Bansari Goshala, says that our aim is to explain the real benefits of cow to the people, people and Gopalak manage it till the time they get cow's milk but do not understand the full importance of cow
 
 vahiin goseva ayog ke adhyaksh dow
